'When I was young I read a story that always stayed with me. It was part of Ursula K. LeGuin\'s Earthsea series, one of the later collections of short stories. I can\'t remember the name now. Briefly, the first woman is allowed to join the wizard college for men but is driven out because of misogyny. To force her to leave they invoke her True Name, the strongest magic in the setting, but she is unique in that it *doesn\'t work*; rather than obey she freezes and screams that is not all that I am!" When pressed her other self emerges, surprising everyone, including her: a dragon. She flies once over the college and its apprehensive wizards, waiting to see if she will destroy them, before wordlessly flying out to sea. My other self is not so grand and powerful as that, but sometimes I flinch when I am called "man" or "him" or "he" it isn\'t a desire to say \'no, I am not a *that*, I am a *this*\' but to echo her cry: \'that is not all that I am, and her time to step out fully has not yet come.\'"',
